         </section>
        </div>
       </header>
       <div class="article rapid-track " data-value="article_body" id="y708-article" itemref="content-header" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
        <div class="article-container" itemprop="articleBody">
         <figure class="article-figure article-hero-figure">
          <img alt="Deaths spark world-wide ice cream recall" class="article-figure-image" itemprop="image" src="https://s.yimg.com/ea/img/-/150421/icecream_1280_1ajbsuq-1ajbtai.jpg?x=656&amp;sig=EvVRSdde6NQxVxz2C2fSwg--"/>
          <figcaption class="article-figure-caption">
           <span class="article-caption-text">
            Deaths spark world-wide ice cream recall
           </span>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
         </p>
         <p class="article-abstract">
          Texas-based Blue Bell Creameries has issued a voluntary worldwide recall for all of its products after two samples of chocolate chip cookie dough ice cream tested positive for listeria, a potentially deadly bacteria.
         </p>
         <p>
          The company "cannot say with certainty" how the bacteria was introduced to its facilities, Blue Bell's chief executive Paul Kruse said in a statement.
         </p>
         <p>
          Blue Bell issued the recall that includes ice cream, frozen yogurt, sherbet and frozen snacks distributed in 23 states and international locations because other products "have the potential to be contaminated," according to the statement.
         </p>
         <p>
          "We're committed to doing the 100 per cent right thing, and the best way to do that is to take all of our products off the market until we can be confident that they are all safe," Kruse said.
         </p>
         <figure class="article-figure ">
          <img class="article-figure-image" src="https://s.yimg.com/dh/ap/default/150420/bluebell2.jpg"/>
          <figcaption class="article-figure-caption">
           <span class="article-figure-source">
            Blue Bell Ice Cream. Photo: AP
           </span>
          </figcaption>
         </figure>
         <p>
          The first recall in the family-owned creamery's 108-year history was issued last month after the U.S. Centers for Disease Control and Prevention linked ice cream contaminated with listeria to three deaths at a Kansas hospital.
         </p>
         <p>
          Five others in Kansas and Texas were sickened with listeriosis, which can cause fever, muscle aches, gastrointestinal symptoms.
         </p>
         <p>
          The illness was tracked to a production line in Brenham, Texas, and later to a second line in Broken Arrow, Oklahoma. The most recently contaminated samples were discovered through a testing program the company initiated after its first recall, according to the statement.
         </p>
         <p>
          Monday's recall extends to retail outlets in Alabama, Arizona, Arkansas, Colorado, Florida, Georgia, Illinois, Indiana, Kansas, Kentucky, Louisiana, Mississippi, Missouri, Nevada, New Mexico, North Carolina, Ohio, Oklahoma, South Carolina, Tennessee, Texas, Virginia, Wyoming and international locations.
         </p>
         <ul>
          <li>
           <a href="//au.news.yahoo.com/world/a/27251948/students-insides-explode-after-taking-diet-pills/">
            Student's insides 'explode' after taking diet pills
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="//au.news.yahoo.com/world/a/27218378/mysterious-worm-rain-stumps-scientists-in-norway/">
            It's raining worms and scientists are baffled
           </a>
          </li>
          <li>
           <a href="//au.news.yahoo.com/world/a/27247968/school-censors-girls-shirt-for-yearbook-photo/">
            School censors 'offensive' feminist shirt
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <p>
          The manufacturing facility in Oklahoma where operations were suspended earlier this month for sanitising will remain closed as Blue Bell continues to investigate the source of the bacteria, the statement said.
         </p>
         <p>
          Blue Bell is implementing a process to test all of its products before releasing them to the market, with plans to resume limited distribution soon.
         </p>
         <p>
          The company said it is also expanding its cleaning and sanitisation system, beefing up its employee training, expanding its swabbing system by 800 per cent to include more surfaces and is sending daily samples to a microbiology laboratory for testing.
         </p>
         <p>
          Listeria primarily affects pregnant women and their newborns, older adults and people with immune systems weakened by cancer, cancer treatments, or other serious conditions.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           News break  April 21
          </strong>

function execY7react()
{
    if (y7react !== undefined &amp;&amp; y7react.modules !== undefined &amp;&amp; Object.keys(y7react.modules).length &amp;&amp; React !== undefined) {
        
        if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
            console.log('Executing react modules');
        }

        for (var moduleIdentifier in y7react.modules) {

            if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                console.log(moduleIdentifier);
            }

            var module = y7react.modules[moduleIdentifier];

            /* check for object to ensure we dont break any further react processing */
            if (window[module.moduleObject]) {

                React.render(
                    React.createElement(window[module.moduleObject], {
                        data: module.data,
                        config: module.config
                    }),
                    document.getElementById(module.moduleId)
                );

            }

            if (y7debug &amp;&amp; console) {
                console.log(module);
            }

        }

        y7react = { modules: {} };

    }
}

    }
}

YUI(y7data.yuiConfig).use(y7jsDeps, function (Y) {
    Y.on('domready', function() {
        execY7modules(Y);
        execY7react();
        execY7System();
    });
});
     </script>
    </div>
    <!-- /div.g-row desktop-layout.html g-row footer content -->
   </div>
   <!-- div.container -->
  </div>
  <!-- div#page -->
 </body>
</html>
